<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:collaborateur.html>collaborateur</a> (28830)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:collaborateur.html>collaborateur</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:word.html>word</a> became <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:primary.html>primary</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:label.html>label</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nazi.html>Nazi</a> collaborators <a href = vnd.unilang:during.html>during</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:second.html>Second</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:world.html>World</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:war.html>War</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:extremely.html>extremely</a> pejorative <a href = vnd.unilang:ever.html>ever</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:since.html>since</a>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:collaborateur.html>collaborateur</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:collaborateurs.html>collaborateurs</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:collaborateur.html>collaborateurtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>One</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:who.html>who</a> collaborates <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> collaborated <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nazis.html>Nazis</a>, fascists <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:another.html>another</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enemy.html>enemy</a>; traitorous collaborator. <span class="defdate">[<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ww.html>Ww</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ii.html>Ii</a>]</span></li>

***colonne.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:colonne.html>colonne</a> (17382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:colonne.html>colonne</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:colonne.html>colonne</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:colonnes.html>colonnes</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:colonne.html>colonnetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:military.html>military</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:column.html>column</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:column.html>column</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:pillar.html>pillar</a>, sile</li></ol>
